implementation is distributed across several key components:\\n\\n## CDS (Cluster Discovery Service) Subscription\\nCluster discovery is managed through three main components in envoyproxy/envoy:\\n\\n1. **CdsApiImpl** (source/common/upstream/cds_api_impl.cc/h) - The main CDS subscription implementation that extends Config::SubscriptionBase<Cluster>. It handles cluster resource subscription, configuration updates via onConfigUpdate(), and failure handling via onConfigUpdateFailed().\\n\\n2. **CdsApiHelper** (source/common/upstream/cds_api_helper.cc/h) - A helper class that processes CDS configuration updates and notifies the cluster manager of cluster additions and removals.\\n\\n3. **OdCdsApiImpl** (source/common/upstream/od_cds_api_impl.cc/h) - On-demand CDS implementation that lazily fetches clusters as needed, with methods like updateOnDemand().\\n\\n4. **ClusterDiscoveryManager** (source/common/upstream/cluster_discovery_manager.cc/h) - Thread-local on-demand cluster discovery manager that invokes discovery callbacks and manages cluster lifecycle callbacks.\\n\\n## Cluster Manager Update Logic\\nThe cluster manager handles dynamic cluster updates through:\\n\\n1. **ClusterManagerImpl** (source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.cc/h) - The main cluster manager implementation with critical methods:\\n   - addOrUpdateCluster() - Adds or updates clusters, managing warming vs. active cluster states\\n   - loadCluster() - Creates cluster instances with proper initialization\\n   - removeCluster() - Removes dynamically added clusters\\n\\n2. **ClusterManagerInitHelper** (source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h) - Manages the complex initialization state machine for primary clusters, secondary clusters, and CDS-populated clusters, with states: Loading, WaitingForPrimaryInitializationToComplete, WaitingToStartSecondaryInitialization, WaitingToStartCdsInitialization, CdsInitialized, and AllClustersInitialized.\\n\\n3. **ClusterFactoryImplBase** (source/common/upstream/cluster_factory_impl.cc/h) - Factory for creating cluster instances from protobuf configurations, coordinating with the outlier detection and health checking subsystems.\\n\\n4. **ClusterUpdateTracker** (source/common/upstream/cluster_update_tracker.cc/h) - Tracks cluster updates and manages the warming-to-active cluster transition.\\n\\n## Cluster Implementation\\nThe base cluster implementation in **upstream_impl.cc/h** contains:\\n- ClusterImplBase - Base class for all cluster implementations with initialization hooks\\n- HostDescriptionImplBase - Host/endpoint representation with health checker and outlier detector integration\\n- Integration points for health checking via setHealthChecker() and setOutlierDetector()\\n\\n## Active Health Check Scheduling\\nHealth checking is implemented across multiple components:\\n\\n1. **Core Health Checking** (source/common/upstream/):\\n   - **HealthCheckerImpl** (health_checker_impl.cc/h) - Factory and base implementation for health checkers\\n   - **HealthCheckerFactory::create()** - Creates appropriate health checker based on configuration\\n   - **HealthDiscoveryService** (health_discovery_service.cc/h) - Service for health discovery subscriptions\\n   - **HealthCheckerEventLogger** (health_checker_event_logger.cc/h) - Logs health check events\\n\\n2. **Health Checker Implementations** (source/extensions/health_checkers/):\\n   - **HealthCheckerBaseImpl** (common/health_checker_base_impl.cc/h) - Base implementation with interval scheduling\\n   - **HttpHealthCheckerImpl** (http/health_checker_impl.cc/h) - HTTP health checking with interval-based probing via onInterval()\\n   - **GrpcHealthCheckerImpl** (grpc/health_checker_impl.cc/h) - gRPC health checking using gRPC.Health.v1 service\\n   - **TcpHealthCheckerImpl** (tcp/health_checker_impl.cc/h) - TCP health checking with payload matching\\n   - **RedisHealthChecker** (redis/redis.cc/h) - Redis protocol health checking\\n   - **ThriftHealthChecker** (thrift/thrift.cc/h) - Thrift protocol health checking\\n\\nHealth checks are scheduled through Event::Dispatcher timers set at intervals defined in HealthCheck configuration protobuf.\\n\\n## Outlier Detection Integration\\nOutlier detection is managed through:\\n\\n1. **OutlierDetectionImpl** (source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.cc/h) -
